1)  
The World of God's Will  
It's a cold day, and I think many of you are quite uncomfortable sitting here. However, from now on, this time that has been granted is as much the teacher's time, so you should understand that you have a responsibility to endure, even if it is difficult.  
I've been talking while touring various districts, so my throat is hoarse. Therefore, it might be quite uncomfortable and hard to listen, so I hope you understand that.  
A person who tries to help others is a true Unification Church member.  
This is Jeonju, Jeollabuk-do, the district headquarters, right? Is that correct? “Yes.” This is a representative place of Jeollabuk-do, but since the district headquarters has not been completed, doesn't that indicate that Jeollabuk-do is incomplete? Although the district headquarters is not completed, what about the people attending here? Are they all completely complete? “I can't hear.”  
I can't hear, so it's a problem. My voice is hoarse, so it's a problem. Is there anything else? Can you hear? “Yes.” I have to hold onto this, but if I do, I can't be free, so it's a problem.  
Now, what I was saying is that Jeonju is the central city of Jeollabuk-do, and since the Unification Church headquarters of Jeonbuk is here, the fact that this church is incomplete means that Jeollabuk-do is incomplete, doesn't it? How about it? “No.”  
So, have you all completed it? Those who came here, can you say, ‘I am not ashamed, there is no one like me in the world, follow my example’? Are you all complete? You are also incomplete, right?  
Bring that here. Can you hear? “Yes.” I have no choice but to do it like this today…. This is not free. “It’s broken.” It’s broken? Why did you bring a broken one today? If this microphone is too high, I can't speak…. Can you hear now? “Yes.”  
I apologize to the gentlemen outside. (Laughter) To speak, I need to look at your faces and make eye contact so that it is good for both the speaker and the listener, but I am very sorry that the environment is not like that. However, since I am standing here, I have no choice but to ask you to quietly listen to what I have to say.  
So, what is the most famous thing in Jeollabuk-do? A person who cannot boast about their hometown is not a person from that hometown. “There is the Honam granary.” The Honam granary! You live right in the middle of the Honam granary, right? What else? “Ilshin Stone.” (Laughter) Ilshin Stone? What else? “The Unification Church.”  
People from Jeolla-do like Jeolla-do the most, right? “Yes.” People from Jeolla-do like Jeolla-do the most, and people from Pyeongan-do like Pyeongan-do the most, right? Therefore, they like Jeolla-do and at the same time like the people from Jeolla-do, right? Isn’t that so? “Yes.” People like us from Pyeongan-do dislike it, right? “No.”  
Why not? “We like it a little less.” So, you like it a little less? (Laughter) Then, will I feel like speaking when I come here? Even if you say you like it, whether I will speak or not depends on that, but if you say you like it a little less, will I feel like speaking? Is that how you treat guests? (Laughter)  
If you say you like it a little less, will I feel good about speaking? You must have answered that way because your words are wrong, your mouth is wrong, but I can only believe that deep down in your hearts, it is not like that. How else could I speak here in Jeolla-do? If you say you like it a little less, then if I say something slightly wrong while speaking, you might feel bad and kick me out, right? (Laughter)  
Now, you Unification Church members in Jeollabuk-do, you are definitely Unification Church members, right? “Yes.” Is it easy or hard to be a Unification Church member? “It’s good.” That is a blatant lie. (Laughter) It is really hard to be a Unification Church member.  
Among Unification Church members, there are true members, and then there are middle members. There are mixed middle members. There are true Unification Church members, then there are middle members, and then there are fake members. So, which category do you all fall into? “True.” Is it true? “Yes.” Are there no middle members? There must be middle members too. There are also fakes. Even if you shout that you are true, I believe that these three types of people have gathered here.  
Who is a true member? A true member is not someone who wants to rely on the Unification Church. A true member is not someone who comes to the Unification Church wanting to receive help. A true member is someone who helps the Unification Church, someone who helps heaven, someone who helps all Unification Church members. The middle member is someone who can receive help from the church if they can, and can also help if they can. Then who is the fake? The fake is someone who comes out to the Unification Church to receive help and rely on it, and if they think there is something good, they come out, and if they think there is nothing good, they retreat. They think the Unification Church can exist for their sake, and if it seems to be a loss to them, they have nothing to do with the Unification Church. Such people can be considered fake members.  
Become a Unification Church member that three generations can follow.  
So, what kind of person will you become? “A true….” A true one? “Yes.” Do you really like it? Since we are on the topic, let’s talk about what it means to be true. What is a true Unification Church member? This is the question. Then who established the Unification Church? “God established it.” Yes, God established it. Since God is invisible, the establishment must be done through visible people. Through whom was it established? “Through the True Parents.” It was established through this not-so-good-looking Mr. Moon. (Laughter)  
Then, for a true Unification Church member to emerge, the leader of the Unification Church, the person who established the Unification Church must be true, right? Am I true? “Yes.” There can be no result without a cause. Is this Mr. Moon, who is always nagging about the Unification Church, a true Unification Church member? That is the question. You are curious whether it is true or fake, right? While ordinary people might advertise and claim something fake is true, a religious leader cannot advertise that they are true even if they are true. That is what a religious leader is. So how do you know? How do you know if it is true or fake? “By looking at what they do….” What they do is such that if it were made like this, is this what true Unification Church members made? (Laughter) That is the problem.  
Therefore, no matter how much people in the world say they are right, that pride will be revealed immediately. Whether it is good or bad, ordinary people can measure it, and those who cannot will fail. To become a religious leader, one cannot know in just one year. One cannot know in one or two years. At least ten years, about thirty years must pass to know whether that religion is right or wrong. Recently, there has been a significant issue surrounding pseudo-religions…  
Moreover, religion cannot be compared to visible objects in terms of size. Therefore, a religious leader cannot be judged at a glance. One cannot say someone is fake just because they are not good-looking, nor can one say someone is true just because they are good-looking. You must understand that. My face is not good-looking, right? “You are good-looking.” What is good-looking about me? You follow around such an ugly person saying, ‘Teacher, Teacher,’ and you don’t realize that it is wrong. Do you understand that? Do you know if I am a liar?  
In the world, everyone is firing cannons, right? Everyone lies for one, two, or three years to deceive the public and make a quick profit. Isn’t that so? That can happen. How do you know if I am such a person? What guarantees that I am not such a person? Do you have confidence in what guarantees it? You cannot answer. Therefore, you cannot stand in a position where you cannot guarantee and judge ‘true or fake.’ Is that so? You must answer. Is it there or not?  
Even if you say, ‘I don’t know whether a Unification Church member is true or fake,’ you cannot answer whether Mr. Moon, who leads the Unification Church and founded it, is a true person or a fake person. Therefore, what is the point of saying anything? Isn’t that so? If you don’t even know that, what use is it for me to speak? “If it’s true, what’s fake…” Who knows if it is true? (Laughter) “You can tell by looking at various things.” How do you know if a red bean is a true red bean or a soybean is a true soybean? You have to plant it to know. Isn’t that so? “Yes.” You plant it, and if you plant red beans, the sprouts come out, and if it grows and flowers, it will surely bear the same red bean fruit; that is a true red bean, and if it is a soybean, it is a true soybean.  
In the same way, by planting the thoughts of Mr. Moon of the Unification Church, the question is whether you will become that true person. Do you understand? “Yes.” If you plant soybeans, the sprouts will come out, and the soybeans will bear fruit. If you plant the thoughts of the Unification Church, you will receive the meaning of the Unification Church, and whether that planted meaning bears fruit and whether you become a true person or not will determine how people evaluate you.  
Therefore, I cannot help but ask, ‘Are you true Unification Church members?’ Is that right? “Yes.” So, are you true Unification Church members? “Yes.” Really? “Yes.” You little rascal! (Laughter) Even if I say such disrespectful words in front of the audience, is it true? “Yes.” Surely, you must become true fruits so that the people of Jeollabuk-do will want to receive the same seeds as Unification Church members. Grandfathers and mothers, their grandchildren, three generations should say, ‘Please, oh, grandchildren, sons, become people like Teacher Moon of the Unification Church. Become Unification Church members, become like Unification Church people.’ If you help each other to set an example, then at that time, it will be possible to say, ‘Ah, those people are indeed true Unification Church members.’ Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.”  
When you walk around your neighborhood, when you go around every nook and cranny of Jeollabuk-do, whether the people in that neighborhood are elderly, middle-aged, or young, they should say, ‘We should follow the Unification Church people. We should follow everything they do. We should follow them in the daytime and in the nighttime, in what they say and in how they live, we should follow their entire behavior. They must absolutely not be absent. Even if there is no village chief, no district chief, no governor of Jeollabuk-do, if we have such people, that’s enough. The people we can follow are those people.’ If that happens, I think they will be the true people needed in Jeollabuk-do. Do you understand? “Yes.”  
Once you believe in a religion, you must change from that day.  
Among you, there are people who might say, ‘I have believed in the Unification Church for 10 years. 20 years.’ I think there are people like that here. It is obvious. Some might say, ‘I have been here for 5 years.’ They say that ten years can change a mountain and river, so if it has been about ten years, a young person who was twenty will become thirty, and a thirty-year-old will become forty, and wrinkles will appear, showing such changes. But if it has been about ten years and you are still stuck in that neighborhood, is this a Unification Church person or what? ‘Look at that guy, what he is doing, it’s the same as before. I heard recently that they believe in a cult called the Unification Church. Hehe.’ (Laughter) Is a person who hears such things a Unification Church member? Can that be considered a true Unification Church member? That is a cult, a heretical religion.  
If you believe in a religion, you must change from that day. How much must you change? You must change as much as the distance between heaven and earth. Do you understand? It is not just a horizontal change; it must change in all directions, vertically as well. That is the path that religion aims for, yet… Many people may have gathered to treat the teacher like this, or perhaps they gathered to prepare a good dinner, but what is most important is this: what has changed in you since you believed in the Unification Church?  
You must understand that what you leave behind for people to follow with absolute certainty is extremely precious. Do you understand? “Yes.”  
A religious leader must receive God's endorsement.  
I do not know whether I am a true person or a fake person, but I have the confidence that even though I am opposed now in South Korea, history will surely not be able to ignore me. I have endured persecution and opposition until now. If there are those who have opposed me until now, they might say, ‘What is true about that?’ But you can only know what is true and what is fake after about thirty years.  
Do you understand what I mean?  
These days, I hear people saying, ‘Well, I thought Mr. Moon was a bad person, but it turns out he is good, they say he is good.’ I have heard rumors from neighboring towns. Some people say, ‘That person is wonderful, and so on.’ Some people even say, ‘Did you meet Mr. Moon?’ ‘I didn’t meet him.’ ‘If you didn’t meet him, just forget it. I met him.’ There are even people who boast about having met him.  
If it has come to that point, I don’t know whether it is good or bad, but the name has been spread. It’s like giving birth to a baby; you give birth, but you don’t know if it’s a girl or a boy. Just as you can only know whether it is a boy or a girl when you lift the bottom up, whether Mr. Moon is a good person or a bad person, he is undoubtedly a problematic figure in South Korea. That is for sure, right? “Yes.” He is undoubtedly a problematic man.  
He was born as a man, but he is a problematic man. We will have to see whether he becomes a traitor or a loyalist… How do we know that? We know by looking at what he does. For one year, two years, ten years, until the end of my life, the good things will remain as good, and the bad things will remain as bad. So, I am a person who is currently trying to become a true person. Whether I have become a true person, I do not know.  
Instead, a religious leader cannot just be someone who is liked by humans based on their arguments. If God exists, the great King of the universe who created heaven and earth must be able to say, ‘Hey, Mr. Moon, you are indeed a true person in the human world.’ That is the endorsement I must receive.

This is the problem.
To do that, you need to have skills and achievements. Do you understand? Skills
Bowing your head in front of someone skilled, and trying to emulate them
is what it means. When you have achievements, you bow your head there. So our 
Unification Church must establish skills and achievements. Although a certain member of the Unification Church is being persecuted and condemned by the established church… The established church members boast about building churches in tall buildings, hanging crosses at the end of the church, and gathering thousands or hundreds of people, but none of that matters to me, it doesn’t matter to me.
Even though the established church pastors oppose the Unification Church, I don’t dislike that. If you want to do it, go ahead. I digest the opposition, and without opposing their opposing words, I naturally subdue them, and if they repent for opposing me in the past, kneel before me, and say they were wrong, then they shouldn’t just ask me for forgiveness, but if they have the heart to ask, they should be more loyal and be able to work more in society, and such a time will come. I believe that those who are opposing now can become loyal subjects in the future. Do you understand what that means? “Yes.”
In that sense, I am thinking of something that transcends this… No matter how much junk and all sorts of things there are, I am busy going my own way without caring about that. Speaking for myself, I feel like I am at a shooting range, concentrating on the target and holding a gun to shoot. But if I get distracted by someone talking next to me, it will cause a lot of trouble.
Last year in Jeonju, during the ‘Day of Hope Grand Festival,’ there was opposition and a commotion, but I didn’t know why that was happening. I wonder if it’s because I became a bad person. Those people are all wonderful… The world is strange. The pastors and elders who are said to be great don’t gather when there are meetings or revivals, but that person from the Unification Church, who is said to be worthless, comes, and why is there a commotion every day in this gymnasium, and why can’t they get in?
Looking at that, it seems that people’s hearts are weighing good and bad. Just like flowers bloom when spring comes… Flowers don’t bloom just because spring comes. When spring comes, flowers naturally bloom, and just like the direction of the earth’s axis finds its way, such actions seem to occur.
When have I ever come to Jeonju to preach? Even though I’ve been here for a few days, seeing so many people gathering is strange. Anyway, rumors have spread. So from now on, keep a close eye on this, starting now. Do you understand? “Yes.” So when will it be decided whether the person called the leader of the Unification Church is real or fake? When? “Tonight.” Tonight at this time? When will it be decided? After death. (Laughter) Isn’t that a sad thing to say? It will be decided after death. After death, whether that person was a patriot or a loyal subject, or what kind of impact they had on this world will be known.
Now, I can influence the United States and Japan. By now, probably the whole world knows me. In America, if someone doesn’t know me, they are not even human. If they are digging a hole in the mountains with wild boars, they might not know, but anyone who listens to the radio or watches television knows Reverend Moon. I have become that famous. Then in Germany or France or Europe, the whole world knows Reverend Moon. Is that good or bad? “Good.” What is good? (Laughter) What is good? Do you get food, do you get rice cakes, do you get clothes? What is good? “Because you are here as a righteous person of God.” How do you know if the teacher is a righteous person?
The people of the world, those Americans are all envious. “Ah, this is from Korea….” When you say Korea, they think of it as a national garbage can, a garbage can. They think that Koreans are people who fight over the rags given to them in America. They think that the people who tear each other apart over relief supplies and clothes are those kinds of people, and they think of it as a garbage can, and they think that the so-called yellow race, with their faces black…
Aren’t you guys more handsome than them? (Laughter) What does that mean? Why are you laughing? It’s not an ugly face. The shape of the face is just okay. To go out into the world, you have to be at least this handsome. (Laughter) If you say you are ugly, it’s disappointing, so you should say you are handsome. It seems you know. The people of Jeolla Province are very quick-witted. (Laughter) I heard that Jeolla Province people know why the neighbor’s dog is barking. Why? Because they are very interested in their neighbors… (Laughter) So when a good guest comes, they want to eat rice cakes when rice cakes are made, and at least get some chicken soup when a chicken is killed. They think they are very interested. If they think about everything centered around themselves, how to go to the neighboring town, then already… That’s how they say it. Isn’t that right? (Someone coughs) What, are you coughing in a bad mood? (Laughter)
That’s why I have become famous. It may be good for the members of the Unification Church, but for the Westerners… When the person known as Reverend Moon from Korea appears, it’s like sitting at the edge of a boat in a storm, it’s more chaotic than that. I have stirred up a whirlwind in America for three years… I know everyone in the media, academia, business, politics, and Congress, including senators. Everyone who is someone knows me.
With this, after stirring up such a whirlwind in America for about three years, the big eyes of the American people have turned upside down… (Laughter. Applause) There’s no time, no time. (Laughter) Their eyes have turned wide open. These big-nosed, big-bodied guys, when a small Asian person appears and shakes things up, it’s like they’ve been hit by a typhoon, shaking their tails and causing a commotion everywhere. When I see that, I hold my nose and go “huh huh.” (Demonstrating. Laughter)
And in the short history of America, I have received 1,200 certificates of commendation. There are names like admiral, general, and many doctors… There are many citizenship certificates as well. If you all want to have one of these later, I can distribute them. (Laughter) This is all a record since the history of America began. So, am I a foolish person or a talented person? “A talented person…” Well, they think I’m a foolish person, but Americans think I’m talented. So you guys have turned around. (Laughter) That’s right, isn’t it? “That’s right!” (Laughter) You’ve turned around.
Here, even though the teacher is alone, as a yellow person, well, I’m not particularly handsome. I may be alone, but when I face 220 million Americans, if I push, it’s not me who gets pushed, it’s them who get pushed. (Laughter) Do you understand? I can go anywhere, even into Congress to give lectures. In the past, I tried to liberate President Nixon, but he didn’t listen, and that’s how it turned out.
Even if you play games, if you were born on the same day and are the same age, you have to wrestle with the big guy to gain something; you won’t gain anything by just following the little ones. Isn’t that right? “That’s right.” This time, I didn’t meet with the top people of the Liberal Democratic Party of Japan. I am selecting the person who will be the Prime Minister of Japan and pushing them forward. Do you understand? If they have something they don’t know, they send someone to ask me. They send a special envoy to ask, “Teacher, what should we do about Japan?” “You fools! Don’t you know? Do it like this and that…” (Laughter)
In the world, they say that a mischievous child at home is a talented child, and a child who acts as a leader in the neighboring town is a foolish child. Isn’t that what they say? “No.” Then what is it? What is real? Is the opposite of what I just said real? “The opposite is real.” The opposite is real? “Yes.” In my family, I am the most foolish one. Even if the country opposes me, and the established church has opposed me for 30 years, I remain quiet, so I am foolish. (Laughter) Where would you find someone as foolish as that? Even if I am foolish, my situation is not that bad. It’s so bad that it doesn’t even count as foolishness. However, when I go abroad, this is the man of the issue. When I say, “You fools!” they say, “Yes.” That’s all it takes. Do you think I’m useful? “Yes.” (Laughter)
Members of the Unification Church need to start with human education.
Even if I come to the Jeonju Unification Church and speak boldly in front of you, I must acknowledge that it is worth saying such things. Huh? “Yes.” What do the ladies and grandmothers know, do they just say “yes”? (Laughter) They probably just practiced this by following their grandchildren. Do they really know and answer? “Yes.” Thank you. (Laughter) Then the young gentlemen standing in the back, do you know? “Yes.” Even if I say something that might be disrespectful to the one who is being insulted, will you forgive me? “Yes.” Even if I say “those bastards”? (Laughter) You have to forgive me even if I curse.
If I come to Jeonju today and experience something that I will never forget in my life, then Jeonju may not be bad. Why? I made this church with the money I earned. Isn’t that right? “Yes.” Did the people of Jeonju gather money? Did the people of Jeolla Province build this church? “No.”
Whose church is this? “Father’s.” What is Father’s church? It’s the Jeolla Province church. (Laughter) It’s not my church; it’s the Jeolla Province church. Isn’t it the Jeolla Province church? When building the Jeolla Province church, shouldn’t the people of Jeolla Province contribute money? Why is a person from Pyeongan Province contributing money? (Laughter) So if I start to think Jeonju is good… Last year, I built hundreds of churches in a hurry. Until now, I’ve been told to suffer and live in shanties with rags… I’ve been treated terribly. The old men in this neighborhood go “pee” and the old women in that neighborhood go “pee” and the uncles go “pee”… I’ve become a top beggar among beggars… But instead, I told the members of the Unification Church to become different people. They are Koreans, but they are not Koreans who are going downhill; they are to become Koreans with hope.
I have also suffered the humiliation of asking a passing young person for a meal, saying, “Please give me a meal.” You know, a household that doesn’t show compassion to beggars is unlucky. Look. When you enter that neighborhood, the true owner of that neighborhood is not the village chief. Who is it? It’s the beggar, the beggar. You might say, “Where is that kind of saying?” but listen. Does the village chief remember the birthdays of all the grandfathers and grandmothers in that neighborhood? Do they remember, or not? “They can’t.” (Laughter) But the beggar remembers the birthdays of all the grandfathers in the neighborhood, down to the grandchildren. Why? (Laughter) Because they are the owner. (Applause) At that time, it would be disrespectful to applaud. They remember every festive day.
Even if a lame person gets married, they know first. Now, whether they are buying rice or mung bean flour to make pancakes or buying beef ribs, they know everything clearly. They don’t miss a thing. And then, they also know when the in-laws from the neighboring town come and go. Is that true or not? “That’s true.” Why is that? Why? Because they are experts at getting free food. (Laughter) When they know that, they don’t envy the rich. Even if the grandfather of a rich family has gone through countless hardships to accumulate wealth, it cannot be compared to their grandfather. Do they eat a feast every day? (Laughter) Do they eat a birthday feast every day? This beggar knows everything about the village, so they might say, “Oh, I don’t see any beggars in this neighborhood today.” But do they know where they went? They went to a feast. They went to a birthday party. The villagers may not know, but they wander around alone… What do they say while wandering alone? “They feast.” They wander around happily. They eat meat and rice to their heart’s content, saying, “Today is my birthday…” (Laughter) And in that neighborhood… “Ah, this house is a good house, this house will be blessed, this house will perish.” They know everything. Do you know that?
That’s why the mouth of a beggar is scary. If a beggar says that house will perish, that house will perish. Why? Because the human heart is bad… Even if it’s not a locked big door, even if it’s a simple door, if that house is said to prosper, it will prosper. Why? Who is the king who knows the human heart? “The beggar.” The beggar. So, our Unification Church members need to conduct human education. We need to educate them about things that ordinary people do not care about, so I sent them all away saying, “The members of the Unification Church across the country should become beggars.”
So, while being chased away, they went to labor sites, went to churches, went to rich houses, went to restaurants, and they have been everywhere. They were trained to learn everything about the social hierarchy of humanity. If you gather all the people who have been sent to Jeollabuk-do from the past to now and say, “Come together,” they can completely sit down and… So, for Jeonju, I investigated all the high-ranking officials, the well-off farmers, and everything. Isn’t that unpleasant? That guy who was wandering around doing foolish things, being insulted, was thought to be a top beggar, someone who would die on the street, but who would have thought he would become like this! He’s a guy who walks around with a badge! What badge? A command badge! (Laughter)
How miserable is that in the history of Korea? Do you understand what I mean? If you don’t treat guests well… “I thought he was a beggar, but I thought he was just a messenger, but it turns out that he is not just the village chief, but even the county governor bows to him.” If that happens, that neighborhood can be completely occupied without any effort. More than occupying, it can be completely subdued. Is that right? Is that right or not? “That’s right.”
So the Unification Church has a lot to say. I have a lot to say, really. If I were to lay it all out, when I unpack the bundle, then people would say, “Oh! I didn’t know anything, but that person is indeed a bit different.” It’s a little different, isn’t it? It’s a little different.
Unification Church members should become people who incur debts wherever they go.
Therefore, just like I mentioned earlier, if I stay quiet while being scolded at home, how pathetic must I be? However, when I go to countries like America, England, or Germany, I get kicked. (Laughter) How pathetic is a Korean person? I may be pathetic, but if you kick my butt, it will break, and if you kick my belly, it will hurt, and if you cut off my head, it will run away… It is because of such things that accidents happen now.

So recently, the American embassy said, "Oh dear, because of Reverend Moon, America has a problem." What problem is there because of Reverend Moon? They don’t know. It’s a problem because there are many bad people, and I am trying to make them good people. Therefore, in a fight, I am not someone who will retreat. The American people are fighting a retreating battle… Is that enough, or not? “That’s enough.” Is that a good person or a bad person? “A good person.” Now, some guy is feeling bad about this… (Laughter) Just wait about seven years and see what I do. Just don’t die for seven years, please, old folks… At that time, you might think, "Oh, when I came to Jeonju, I should have greeted him warmly and exchanged business cards, introduced our son-in-law or our grandchildren." That might be possible.

So look at yourselves, look at the Unification Church itself… I don’t know what kind of guy this district leader is. By looking at this guy, the district members will know what kind of people they are. Also, this guy knows whether the people attending church services are real or fake. Is that right? Therefore, preaching is necessary. If you have this kind of thought, the Unification Church will sweep the world in an instant. The world will quickly become all our side. Do you think that will happen?

Since the spring season is a woman's season, the new spring must be welcomed by women. Now look at the world ten years from now; what will happen? The democratic world ten years from now will be a mess, and the communist world ten years from now will also be a mess. However, the world of the Unification Church ten years from now will not be a mess. Once individual perfection is achieved, it leads to family perfection, tribal perfection.... It will continue to develop without collapsing. It goes in a straight line. In the past, it went up and down, zigzagging and doing all sorts of things. But now it is a straight line. Is that not certain? "It is certain."

Therefore, as the cosmic spring day that can match this heaven and earth approaches, to have participated in the march toward Yankee Stadium, waving the flag to become the first protagonist welcoming spring is a miraculous, cosmic miracle. The march command must be a historical command of the world, and the speed of the advancing line must be the speed of a historical line of the world. That goes without saying.

Is New York starting to collapse now, or not? "It's starting to collapse." Here, we must completely revive New York. So, we want to make it a New York that has welcomed the new spring. Since the members of the Unification Church have welcomed spring, the environment must also become spring. That is what we are making. The spring festival for all American citizens is the Yankee Stadium event. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

Going to the Washington event to welcome summer, and then on the day we go to the Moscow event, winter will transition into spring and summer, and the world will become one world. That is how it looks. So, you will become the prince of spring. What will you become? "Prince." Prince. Yes, do you like being a prince? "Yes." Will women win, or will men win? A prince or a princess? "Prince." Princess or princess! "Prince (the men)." Why is that? It is because of the principle. In restoration, women are meant to welcome spring first. (Applause)

Unification Church women are the strongest. They are stronger than men. "Stronger than God. Stronger than the teacher." It must be like this. (Laughter) Otherwise, they will fall again. Can that be so? "Yes." Then what will men do? Do women give birth to babies, or do men give birth to babies? (Laughter) When singing, do women suddenly come to mind, or do men suddenly come to mind? Women's singing voices are higher, or men's singing voices are higher? "Women." Men are only like bass. "Wow." (Laughter) They don't go up. The high and sharp ones are still women. Does it hurt more when a man stabs, or when a woman stabs? "Women." That's right. There are many phenomena in laughter, and that is women. "Hehehe" "Hohoho," but men only have one kind, "Hehehe." (Laughter)

So, is God a simple God or a diverse God? "A diverse God." When given something, men just say, "That's good." But women express it richly and diversely with their mouths and eyes.... (Imitating) Which one shows more expressions of liking? In that sense, when it comes to welcoming spring, when asked who wants to do it first, men are dull and do not understand spring well. Women are sensitive. As soon as spring comes, they want to go out. (Laughter)

Now, as the cosmic spring is coming, will we only welcome spring in the morning, or will we do it in the daytime, or at night? "At night...." Or will we do it on a moonlit night? Which night do you prefer, a dark night or a moonlit night? "Moonlit night." True lovers prefer to go where others cannot see them and enjoy themselves. They prefer the dark night. You must understand that. So, we must also play in spring at night.

That is why we must play in spring even while sleeping. Since we cannot avoid sleeping, we should welcome spring even while sleeping. While sleeping, let’s say, "Hmm, hmm, hmm," and even in dreams, let's welcome spring. Then, when we wake up, let’s cover ourselves with a blanket and try to welcome spring at night. Who would refuse that? God would be pleased to see it, wouldn't He? Is there anything that does not smile in spring? Everything smiles. Spring is when heaven lowers itself, and everything around wants to embrace me warmly, and it is the time when I want to sing even while sleeping.

Therefore, the spring season is a woman's season. The autumn season is a man's season. Until now, in the fallen world, it was the time to create men, so women moved the world without names, but in the new ideal age to come, women will take the lead. 

In the Yankee Stadium event, both the East and the West must not lose. So where should spring first come to this world? Is it the West or the East?
Is it so? Is the West ahead, or is the East ahead? "The East." Why? Why is that? These Westerners have made the West ahead and have not let the East fall behind, so why has the East been ahead and the West fallen behind? Have you thought about that? Why is that? That is the principle of heaven and earth.

Therefore, the conclusion is that the West must follow the East. So where does spring begin? From the East. Then, where did today's Unification Church come from? Did it come from America? "Korea." When you say 'Korea,' it becomes the word 'career' in English, right? Do you like Korea? "Yes." Do you like the East? "Yes." Why? Why? Because Reverend Moon is here. If Reverend Moon were not here, what would Korea or the East matter? Is that right, or not? "That's right."

Looking at this, in any case, the West will follow after a day or two. Therefore, we must become one. The East must also become spring, and indeed the West, including America, can also become spring; this movement is a cosmic inclination. It is what God likes, what our ancestors liked, what humanity living on this earth today likes, and what our descendants will like. We want to welcome this tremendous cosmic spring.

So will you be able to welcome spring well or not? "We will." Will you be happy and laugh, sweating and loving it to death? "We will love it to death." You must love it to the point of being out of your mind.

So we must search every nook and cranny of New York. There is no place where spring does not go. Can we say, "Let's stop at the Harlem area of the Negro community, let's stop at the Spanish community, and only go to the white community"? "No." If an American says that, then that American is wrong, and if a white person says that, then that white person is also wrong. That is not welcoming spring. Therefore, spring must go everywhere. Since we have brought the flag of spring and the news of spring, we must be able to welcome spring normally, and will you do that? Those who want to do that, raise your hands. Ah! Beautiful! Wonderful! (Laughter)

So far, the 20 days we promised have passed. Last night, I gathered the Japanese members and declared, "This Yankee Stadium event will be the responsibility of the Japanese members." Why? Because spring must come from the East. Do Westerners welcome it? Do white people, Americans, welcome it or not? "They do not welcome it." Then what will you do? You are the owners; do you want to act like the owners or like guests? "We are the owners."

So are you guests, or are the Japanese guests? "The Japanese are guests." If all the Japanese guests sweep everything away, then you have no qualification as owners. Will that happen? "No." Japanese people wake up at five o'clock, while Americans wake up at eight o'clock; is that okay? "No." Americans are tall, so they can cover the distance that takes Japanese people three steps in one step, right? Yesterday, I said, "You Japanese people have no cars, so you must take bus number 11." But American friends have cars, so in the morning, if they go 'vroom,' they can cover the distance that takes Japanese people an hour in ten minutes... (Laughter) Since you have cars, can't you take it slow? "No."

So if you go ahead with a car here and go ahead with bus number 11, who is greater? "The Japanese." Then will you throw away all the cars you have? Can you run without a car? "Yes." The Japanese have practiced until now, but you have not practiced, so you must run, right? Can you run? Therefore, you will lose unless you make several times the effort of the Japanese. You might think, "The Japanese can't even speak properly, so how can they beat Americans? We will win." But do not say such things. If you do, you will lose. What will happen when you lose? Therefore, last night, I told the Americans to challenge us. Challenge us. Will you lose here, or will you win? "We will win."

It is already 2:10. I came here saying I would talk for only two hours, but since I have exceeded ten minutes, my mother is now saying, "Why aren't you keeping your promise?" So I have no choice but to stop talking. "No." My mother is now full. (Laughter) You are all young men, so you do not understand the situation well, but I know well. You feel sympathy for them, right? "Yes." These ones (to the men) are not even human. (Laughter)

So understand this... America is a leading advanced country in the democratic world, and Japan fought and won during the Greater East Asia War, so what is there to lose here? Also, the Japanese lost at that time, so this time they must win. Therefore, I say to try it. (Applause. Laughter)

You might think, "The teacher should support us because he is an Eastern person and will side with Japan." Will you say, "I will support the Japanese from a normal standpoint"? What will you do if I say, "Do well, Japan"? I must do it in multiples. If we fight more fiercely, will we get more fierce results or not? "We will." That is a good thing, a good thing. So will you lose to the Japanese, or not? "We will not lose." Will the Japanese lose or not? "They will not lose." I will watch. I am just observing like this.

To win at the Yankee Stadium event, you must engage in organized activities. Therefore, starting today, what will you do? *Kamiya! From now on, we must urgently organize... There are only 44 days left. To extend the victory of the Madison Square Garden event to the Yankee Stadium event, we must engage in even more dazzling activities. (*Speaking in Japanese to Mr. Kamiya) Now everyone must worry about the Yankee Stadium event; not worrying is a big problem. Not worrying is a big problem. Even if we work ten times harder than during the Madison Square Garden event, we are acting more complacently than then. If that is the case, we will not even be able to gather to the standards of the Madison Square Garden event.

You say you cannot evangelize because there are no flyers or leaflets, but what are flyers? My fist, my eyes, and my body are all billboards and leaflets. We do not need the Bicentennial Seal or designs or commemorative advertisements. My spirit, my hands, my actions, and my mouth surpass any poster. *Pour your passion into that. Try to do it like crazy. It is okay even if it is painful to act. Let them criticize. There will be more effect than not being criticized. From today, we must solidify our hearts through New York and act with a firm heart. From now on, we must wake up at five-thirty. You must wake up then. (*Speaking in Japanese)

You only need to sleep two hours a day. You sleep like others, do things like others, and yet when do you restore this world? With such thoughts, you must now organize. From today, you must organize a structure similar to the overall Madison Square Garden event so that Kamiya can command from the headquarters... The executives must meet in one place in the morning and receive reports in the evening, and then contact the teacher, even if it is through a phone call, and must report! Is Neil here? Reiner and everyone must live together, eat, and sleep together. They must eat and sleep at one table. *Wake up in the morning, set plans, and until you return in the evening... The top executives must receive reports and give detailed instructions daily to set the standards for the victorious Yankee Stadium event. You must run around and do it even more than during the Yeouido National Restoration World Assembly, and for the next 44 days, you must digest this as a victorious period. (*Speaking in Japanese)

Gather all the workers who were at Belvedere with that microphone, and everyone must cooperate this time. Those who do not move in front of the teacher have no need to be here. So just get lost. Go somewhere else. The same goes for the American members' wives. If the husbands have gathered, the wives should follow, but they should follow to do the same work. Women must do more than men. During the restoration period, they must do even more. And by the end of this gathering, we must organize so that we can completely clean up without leaving a trace.

Mr. Park is the same. We must all unite and launch a total attack. The same goes for the teacher. I will never become a leader who owes you. I will lead a busier life than you, care more than you, and worry more than you.

I would like to lead directly in the middle of New York, but there are many enemies. They think that if they just kill Reverend Moon, this Unification Church will break apart, and all the problems in America will disappear. I have received quite a few reports like that. Therefore, it is unfavorable for the teacher to appear before the public. It is strategically unfavorable. Do you think so? "Yes."

So you must do it in my place. You must do a hundred or a thousand times more than what the teacher would do in the streets. You must understand that you have that duty. In return, I will surely be at the forefront in the spiritual world. So now I am thinking of not holding the Belvedere gathering anymore. Now we will deploy at seven o'clock. Do you understand what I mean? Huh? "Yes." However, if the cleaning operation starts, we must deploy at six-thirty and go until seven-thirty. For 40 days, you will not die if you do not sleep. You will not die if you do not eat. So there should be no objections.

You, the American members, must establish a historical tradition in this work... Look. We must solemnly declare that we will establish a historical tradition. You must understand that you should voluntarily declare it.

So, will you decide for yourselves? "Yes." Do it. In the name of God! In the name of humanity! In the name of True Parents! I ask that you become victorious. Will you do that? Answer me. "Yes." *
